Erleichtern Sie sich die Arbeit vor Ort mit dem leistungsstärksten Entwurfs- und Überarbeitungswerkzeug. \r\n\r\nDie AutoCAD mobile-Mobilgeräte-App bietet viele Funktionen und Möglichkeiten. Sie können 2D-DWG-Zeichnungen direkt von der Festplatte, aus E-Mails oder externem Speicher hochladen und öffnen und alle Funktionen der DWG-Datei nutzen, z. B. externe Referenzen, Layer und Bildunterlagen. Führen Sie ein Upgrade auf AutoCAD mobile Premium durch, um die Bearbeitungs- und Zeichenwerkzeuge nutzen zu können. Ob Sie online oder offline, im Büro oder vor Ort arbeiten: Sie entwerfen jedes Detail, an jedem Ort. \r\n\r\nOb Sie eine DWG-Datei entwerfen, anzeigen oder markieren möchten: AutoCAD mobile bietet den passenden Plan. \r\n\r\nFunktionen:\r\n\r\n• Kostenloser Test der Premium-Edition für neue Benutzer ohne Verpflichtung\r\n• Öffnen und Anzeigen von DWG-Dateien\r\n• Genaue Messungen vor Ort\r\n• Multi-Touch-Zoom und Schwenken zur einfachen Navigation in großen Zeichnungen\r\n• Offline arbeiten und Änderungen online synchronisieren\r\n• Externer Cloud-Speicher: Zeichnungen von Google Drive, Dropbox, OneDrive usw. anzeigen\r\n• Entwürfe über Mobilgeräte direkt für andere freigeben \r\n• Plotten Sie Entwürfe als PDF, und geben Sie sie über E-Mail frei.\r\n• Laden Sie Konstruktionen als DWG oder DXF oder PDF auf Ihre lokale Festplatte herunter \r\n• Mit der zugehörigen kostenlosen Web-App schnell über den Browser auf Zeichnungen zugreifen\r\n\r\nVorteile einer AutoCAD mobile Premium Subscription:\r\n\r\n• Erstellen neuer Zeichnungen\r\n• Unterstützung größerer Dateien und mehr Speicherkapazität\r\n• Alle Zeichen- und Bearbeitungswerkzeuge, einschließlich erweiterter Werkzeuge wie z. B. Bogen, Versatz und mehr! \r\n• Zeichnen und Bearbeiten von Formen mit höchster Genauigkeit dank Objektfang und neuer Tastenfeldfunktion \r\n• Wählen, Verschieben, Drehen und Skalieren von is one of the most played board games in the world, play with your friends, try to defeat your opponents with strategy, reasoning and a little bit of luck.\r\nGeneral rules of dominoes:\r\n- Blocking game\r\nThe most basic dominos variant is for two players and requires a double six set. The 28 domino tiles are shuffled face down and form the stock or boneyard. Each player draws seven tiles; the remainder are not used. Once the players begin drawing tiles, they are typically placed on-edge before the players, so that each player can see his own domino tiles, but none can see the value of other players' tiles. Every player can thus see how many tiles remain in the other players' hands at all times during gameplay. One player begins by downing (playing the first tile) one of their tiles. In different games first tiles are also different. In Muggins player should start with the highest double (6-6), in Bergen the first move should be 0-0, in Mexican train each round starts with the next lower double. This tile starts the line of play, a series of tiles in which adjacent tiles touch with matching, i.e. equal, values. The players alternately extend the line of play with one tile at one of its two ends. The game ends when one player wins by playing their last tile, or when the game is blocked because neither player can play. If that occurs, whoever caused the block gets all of the remaining player points not counting their own.\r\n- Scoring game\r\nPlayers accrue points during game play for certain configurations, moves, or emptying one's hand. Most scoring games use variations of the draw game. In Muggins (All fives) player must make the open ends of the layout add up to 5s or a multiple of five (5s, 10, 15, 20, etc.) In bergen player scores when numbers on the open ends are equal. If a player does not call \"domino\" before the tile is laid on the table, and another player says 'domino' after the tile is laid, the first player must pick up an extra domino. In Mexican train the double zero domino is scored as 50 points.\r\n- Draw game\r\nIn a draw game (blocking or scoring), players are additionally allowed to draw as many tiles as desired from the stock before playing a tile. The score of a game is the number of pips in the losing player's hand plus the number of pips in the stock. Most rules prescribe that two tiles need to remain in the stock. The Draw game is often referred to as simply \"dominos\".\r\n\r\nIf you like board games like Checkers, Mahjong, Backgammon and Chess, you will love Dominoes: Best Classic Dominoes Board Game.","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9MT92N26MHFR","TileLayout":"Poster","Title":"Golf Battle 3D","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.5307.13816880243720198.8f2ef58f-d174-4da1-9896-2d1fd38f09fe.fac5a049-8540-4df0-9597-4d158b032e33","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"#FFFFFF","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.26914.13816880243720198.8f2ef58f-d174-4da1-9896-2d1fd38f09fe.d95ca052-2326-48d8-9849-a96506bbf23a","Height":300,"Width":620,"BackgroundColor":"#FFFFFF","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Kostenlos","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":0.0,"RatingsCount":"0","PackageFamilyNames":["44511HappyDragonInc.GolfBattle3D_ffz6r8qf25722"],"ContentIds":["31a5fb02-31ab-2387-3549-9a221dc60e85","71a746dd-1690-1dfa-2502-2a75c8579985"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Golf Battled 3D - Join the most exciting Golf ever!
